       <h2 class="vtmn-my-4 vtmn-typo_title-4">Ça peut vous intéresser</h2>

       <div class="vtmn-my-4 gt-tablet:vtmn-w-full svelte-1a89mmc carousel-container">

        <div class="slider svelte-17gwspz">

         <div class="slides svelte-17gwspz" style="" aria-valuenow="0" aria-valuemin="0" aria-valuemax="5" role="list">

          <section class="slide fluid dkt-item svelte-17gwspz active snap" role="listitem">
